class="nav-dropdown-icon w-icon-dropdown-toggle"></div></div><nav class="dropdown-list-mobile w-dropdown-list"><div class="theme-mobile"><div><a href="/about" class="clicable-links-pages w-inline-block"><h5 class="nav-bar-secondary-page is-dark-blue space-right-8px">About Moloco</h5></a></div></div><div class="theme-mobile"><div><a href="/careers" class="clicable-links-pages w-inline-block"><h5 class="nav-bar-secondary-page is-dark-blue space-right-8px">Careers</h5></a></div></div><div class="theme-mobile"><div><a href="/newsroom" class="clicable-links-pages space-top-40px w-button">Contact us</a></div></div></div><main class="cr-main-wrapper"><section class="cr-hero cr-micro"><div class="js w-embed w-script"><script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/gsap@3.12.5/dist/gsap.min.js"></script>

<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {

  const MAX = 11;
  const DURATION = 0.7;
  const STEP_DELAY = 0.3;
  const EASE = "power2.inOut";
  const FADE_DURATION = 0.25;
  const EXTRA_ON_REPEAT = STEP_DELAY * 0.5;
  const PERIOD = STEP_DELAY + DURATION;
  const MOVE_CIRCLE = 110;
  const MOVE_TEXT = 100;
  const IMAGE_LEAD = 0.4;

  const COLORS = [
    "#CCF5E8", "#E8C4FD", "#CDC2FF", "#73E4FF", "#CCF5E8",
    "#E8C4FD", "#CDC2FF", "#73E4FF", "#CCF5E8", "#CCF5E8"
  ];

  const imageGroups = new Map();
  for (let i = 1; i <= MAX; i++) {
    const list = document.querySelectorAll(`[cr-anim="image-${i}"]`);
    if (list && list.length) imageGroups.set(i, list);
  }

  let currentImageIndex = 1;
  let flipCall = null;

  function killTweens(group) {
    group && group.forEach(el => gsap.killTweensOf(el));
  }

  function instantState(el, show) {
    const t = el.style.transition;
    el.style.transition = "none";
    el.style.display = show ? "block" : "none";
    el.style.opacity = show ? "1" : "0";
    void el.offsetHeight;
    el.style.transition = t || "";
  }

  function showOnly(index) {
    imageGroups.forEach((group, num) => {
      group.forEach(el => instantState(el, num === index));
    });
    currentImageIndex = index;
  }

  showOnly(1);

  function showImageByNumber(n) {
    const clamped = Math.max(1, Math.min(MAX, n));
    if (clamped === currentImageIndex) return;

    const prevGroup = imageGroups.get(currentImageIndex);
    const nextGroup = imageGroups.get(clamped);
    if (!nextGroup) return;

    const isLoopReset = currentImageIndex === MAX && clamped === 1;
    if (isLoopReset) {
      showOnly(1);
      return;
    }

    killTweens(prevGroup);
    killTweens(nextGroup);

    if (prevGroup) {
      prevGroup.forEach(el => {
        gsap.to(el, {
          opacity: 0,
          duration: FADE_DURATION,
          ease: "power1.out",
          onComplete: () => { el.style.display = "none"; }
        });
      });
    }

    nextGroup.forEach(el => {
      el.style.display = "block";
      el.style.opacity = "0";
      gsap.to(el, { opacity: 1, duration: FADE_DURATION, ease: "power1.out" });
    });

    currentImageIndex = clamped;
  }

  function createLoop(prefix, moveValue, onStep, { onCycle } = {}) {
    const items = [];
    for (let i = 1; i <= MAX; i++) {
      const el = document.querySelector(`[cr-anim="${prefix}-${i}"]`);
      if (el) items.push(el);
    }

    gsap.set(items, { yPercent: 0 });

    const steps = items.length - 1;
    const tl = gsap.timeline({ repeat: -1 });

    for (let i = 0; i < steps; i++) {
      const offset = i === 0 ? `+=${STEP_DELAY}` : `+=${PERIOD}`;
      tl.to([items[i], items[i + 1]], {
        yPercent: `-=${moveValue}`,
        duration: DURATION,
        ease: EASE,
        onStart: () => { if (onStep) onStep(i + 1); }
      }, offset);
    }

    tl.eventCallback("onRepeat", () => {
      gsap.set(items, { yPercent: 0 });
      if (flipCall) { flipCall.kill(); flipCall = null; }
      showOnly(1);
      if (typeof onCycle === "function") onCycle();
      tl.pause();
      gsap.delayedCall((STEP_DELAY * 2) + EXTRA_ON_REPEAT, () => tl.play());
    });

    return tl;
  }

  const wrapper = document.querySelector('[cr-anim="wrapper"]');

  createLoop("circle", MOVE_CIRCLE, null);

  createLoop("text", MOVE_TEXT, stepIndex => {
    if (wrapper) {
      gsap.to(wrapper, { backgroundColor: COLORS[stepIndex % COLORS.length], duration: 1, ease: EASE });
    }
    const when = Math.max(0, DURATION - IMAGE_LEAD);
    if (flipCall) { flipCall.kill(); flipCall = null; }
    flipCall = gsap.delayedCall(when, () => showImageByNumber(stepIndex + 1));
  }, {
    onCycle: () => showOnly(1)
  });

});
</script></div><div class="cr-hero_container consumer-micro"><div class="cr-hero_content cr-micro"><div class="cr-hero_text cr-micro"><h1 class="cr-hero_heading cr-text-light bigger desktop">Find new <br/></h1><div class="cr-hero_first"><div class="cr-hero_vertical-anim"><div cr-anim="wrapper" class="cr-vertical_left"><div cr-anim="text-1" class="cr-vertical_text-wrapper"><div class="cr-vertical_text">Shopping app</div></div><div cr-anim="text-2" class="cr-vertical_text-wrapper absolute"><div class="cr-vertical_text">Delivery app</div></div><div cr-anim="text-3" class="cr-vertical_text-wrapper absolute"><div class="cr-vertical_text">Food &amp; Drink app</div></div><div cr-anim="text-4" class="cr-vertical_text-wrapper absolute"><div class="cr-vertical_text">Entertainment app</div></div><div cr-anim="text-5" class="cr-vertical_text-wrapper absolute"><div class="cr-vertical_text">Finance app</div></div><div cr-anim="text-6" class="cr-vertical_text-wrapper absolute"><div class="cr-vertical_text">Travel app</div></div><div cr-anim="text-7" class="cr-vertical_text-wrapper absolute"><div class="cr-vertical_text">Retail app</div></div><div cr-anim="text-8" class="cr-vertical_text-wrapper absolute"><div class="cr-vertical_text">Wellness app</div></div><div cr-anim="text-9" class="cr-vertical_text-wrapper absolute"><div class="cr-vertical_text">Dating app</div></div><div cr-anim="text-10" class="cr-vertical_text-wrapper absolute"><div class="cr-vertical_text">Shopping app</div></div></div><div class="cr-vertical_right"><div cr-anim="circle-7" class="cr-vertical_icon-custom absolute w-embed"><svg viewBox="0 0 72 72" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
